# Mastercrafted handout catalog

Auto-generated by `scripts/gen-mastercrafted-handouts.py`. 
Re-run after DB changes.

How to hand items out:

- **To yourself**: `/summonitem <item_id>` &mdash; summons one of the item into your bags.
- **To yourself, into the bank**: `/summonitem <item_id> 1 bank`.
- **Directly to another player**: `/giveitem <player_name> <item_id>`.
- **Give yourself coin**: `/player coins add plat 100` (or gold/silver/copper).

Level shown is the item's required/recommended level. 
Items at level 1 have no requirement set in the DB.

---
